{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01Wpy39nCX798KrwsxEx5pqN","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→//! File-based locking for concurrent write safety in beads_zig.\n     2→//!\n     3→//! Uses POSIX flock (or LockFileEx on Windows) for process-level locking.\n     4→//! The lock is automatically released when the process terminates (kernel-managed).\n     5→//!\n     6→//! Stale lock detection:\n     7→//! - PID is written to lock file after acquisition\n     8→//! - Before blocking on a held lock, we check if the holder PID is still alive\n     9→//! - If the holder process is dead, we break the stale lock safely\n    10→//!\n    11→//! Write path: flock(LOCK_EX) -> write PID -> operation -> flock(LOCK_UN) (~1ms)\n    12→//! Lock is blocking by default, with optional timeout.\n    13→\n    14→const std = @import(\"std\");\n    15→const builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n    16→const test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n    17→\n    18→pub const LockError = error{\n    19→    LockFailed,\n    20→    LockTimeout,\n    21→    FileNotFound,\n    22→    AccessDenied,\n    23→    Unexpected,\n    24→    StaleLockBroken,\n    25→};\n    26→\n    27→pub const BeadsLock = struct {\n    28→    file: std.fs.File,\n    29→    path: []const u8,\n    30→\n    31→    const Self = @This();\n    32→\n    33→    /// Default timeout for stale lock detection (30 seconds).\n    34→    pub const DEFAULT_STALE_TIMEOUT_MS: u64 = 30_000;\n    35→\n    36→    /// Acquire exclusive lock. Blocks until available.\n    37→    /// If the lock is held by a dead process, breaks the stale lock.\n    38→    /// The lock is automatically released when the BeadsLock is deinitialized\n    39→    /// or when release() is called.\n    40→    pub fn acquire(path: []const u8) LockError!Self {\n    41→        return acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path, DEFAULT_STALE_TIMEOUT_MS);\n    42→    }\n    43→\n    44→    /// Acquire exclusive lock with stale lock detection and timeout.\n    45→    /// If the lock holder process is dead, the lock is broken and acquired.\n    46→    /// Returns error.LockTimeout if timeout_ms elapses without acquiring.\n    47→    pub fn acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path: []const u8, timeout_ms: u64) LockError!Self {\n    48→        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n    49→        errdefer file.close();\n    50→\n    51→        // Try non-blocking lock first\n    52→        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n    53→        if (locked) {\n    54→            // Got the lock immediately - write our PID\n    55→            writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n    56→            return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n    57→        }\n    58→\n    59→        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n    60→        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n    61→            if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n    62→                // Holder is dead - force acquire by blocking\n    63→                // The kernel will grant us the lock since the holder is gone\n    64→                lockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n    65→                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n    66→                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n    67→            }\n    68→        }\n    69→\n    70→        // Holder is alive or PID unknown - wait with timeout\n    71→        const start = std.time.milliTimestamp();\n    72→        const deadline = start + @as(i64, @intCast(timeout_ms));\n    73→\n    74→        while (std.time.milliTimestamp() < deadline) {\n    75→            const try_locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n    76→            if (try_locked) {\n    77→                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n    78→                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n    79→            }\n    80→\n    81→            // Check if holder died while we were waiting\n    82→            if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n    83→                if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n    84→                    // Holder died - try to acquire\n    85→                    const dead_locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n    86→                    if (dead_locked) {\n    87→                        writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n    88→                        return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n    89→                    }\n    90→                }\n    91→            }\n    92→\n    93→            // Sleep briefly before retrying\n    94→            std.Thread.sleep(10 * std.time.ns_per_ms);\n    95→        }\n    96→\n    97→        file.close();\n    98→        return LockError.LockTimeout;\n    99→    }\n   100→\n   101→    /// Try to acquire lock without blocking.\n   102→    /// Returns null if lock is held by another process.\n   103→    pub fn tryAcquire(path: []const u8) LockError!?Self {\n   104→        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n   105→        errdefer file.close();\n   106→\n   107→        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n   108→        if (!locked) {\n   109→            file.close();\n   110→            return null;\n   111→        }\n   112→\n   113→        // Got the lock - write our PID\n   114→        writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n   115→\n   116→        return .{\n   117→            .file = file,\n   118→            .path = path,\n   119→        };\n   120→    }\n   121→\n   122→    /// Try to acquire lock, breaking stale locks from dead processes.\n   123→    /// Returns null if lock is held by a live process.\n   124→    pub fn tryAcquireBreakingStale(path: []const u8) LockError!?Self {\n   125→        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n   126→        errdefer file.close();\n   127→\n   128→        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n   129→        if (locked) {\n   130→            writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n   131→            return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n   132→        }\n   133→\n   134→        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n   135→        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n   136→            if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n   137→                // Holder is dead - force acquire\n   138→                lockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n   139→                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n   140→                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n   141→            }\n   142→        }\n   143→\n   144→        // Holder is alive\n   145→        file.close();\n   146→        return null;\n   147→    }\n   148→\n   149→    /// Acquire with timeout (in milliseconds).\n   150→    /// Returns null if lock could not be acquired within timeout.\n   151→    /// DEPRECATED: Use acquireWithStaleLockDetection instead for better stale lock handling.\n   152→    pub fn acquireTimeout(path: []const u8, timeout_ms: u64) LockError!?Self {\n   153→        const result = acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path, timeout_ms) catch |err| {\n   154→            if (err == LockError.LockTimeout) {\n   155→                return null;\n   156→            }\n   157→            return err;\n   158→        };\n   159→        return result;\n   160→    }\n   161→\n   162→    /// Check if this lock file appears to be held by a dead process.\n   163→    /// This is informational only - use tryAcquireBreakingStale to actually acquire.\n   164→    pub fn isStale(path: []const u8) bool {\n   165→        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return false;\n   166→        defer file.close();\n   167→\n   168→        // Try to get lock - if we can, it's not held at all\n   169→        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return false;\n   170→        if (locked) {\n   171→            unlock(file) catch {};\n   172→            return false; // Not held, so not stale\n   173→        }\n   174→\n   175→        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n   176→        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n   177→            return !isProcessAlive(holder_pid);\n   178→        }\n   179→\n   180→        // Can't determine PID, assume not stale\n   181→        return false;\n   182→    }\n   183→\n   184→    /// Get the PID of the current lock holder, if available.\n   185→    pub fn getHolderPid(path: []const u8) ?i32 {\n   186→        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return null;\n   187→        defer file.close();\n   188→        return readPidFromLockFile(file);\n   189→    }\n   190→\n   191→    /// Release the lock.\n   192→    pub fn release(self: *Self) void {\n   193→        // Clear PID before releasing (optional, but clean)\n   194→        self.file.seekTo(0) catch {};\n   195→        self.file.setEndPos(0) catch {};\n   196→\n   197→        unlock(self.file) catch {};\n   198→        self.file.close();\n   199→    }\n   200→\n   201→    /// Deinitialize and release lock.\n   202→    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n   203→        self.release();\n   204→    }\n   205→};\n   206→\n   207→/// Execute a function while holding the beads lock.\n   208→/// Provides RAII-style lock management.\n   209→pub fn withLock(path: []const u8, comptime func: fn () anyerror!void) !void {\n   210→    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(path);\n   211→    defer lock.release();\n   212→    return func();\n   213→}\n   214→\n   215→/// Execute a function with context while holding the beads lock.\n   216→pub fn withLockContext(\n   217→    path: []const u8,\n   218→    context: anytype,\n   219→    comptime func: fn (@TypeOf(context)) anyerror!void,\n   220→) !void {\n   221→    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(path);\n   222→    defer lock.release();\n   223→    return func(context);\n   224→}\n   225→\n   226→// Platform-specific implementations\n   227→\n   228→fn openOrCreateLockFile(path: []const u8) !std.fs.File {\n   229→    const dir = std.fs.cwd();\n   230→\n   231→    // Ensure parent directory exists\n   232→    if (std.fs.path.dirname(path)) |parent| {\n   233→        dir.makePath(parent) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   234→            error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n   235→            else => return err,\n   236→        };\n   237→    }\n   238→\n   239→    // Open or create the lock file\n   240→    return dir.createFile(path, .{\n   241→        .read = true,\n   242→        .truncate = false,\n   243→        .lock = .none, // We handle locking separately\n   244→    });\n   245→}\n   246→\n   247→fn lockExclusive(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n   248→    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n   249→        try lockExclusiveWindows(file);\n   250→    } else {\n   251→        try lockExclusivePosix(file);\n   252→    }\n   253→}\n   254→\n   255→fn tryLockExclusive(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n   256→    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n   257→        return tryLockExclusiveWindows(file);\n   258→    } else {\n   259→        return tryLockExclusivePosix(file);\n   260→    }\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→fn unlock(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n   264→    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n   265→        try unlockWindows(file);\n   266→    } else {\n   267→        try unlockPosix(file);\n   268→    }\n   269→}\n   270→\n   271→// POSIX implementation using flock\n   272→fn lockExclusivePosix(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n   273→    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.EX) catch {\n   274→        return error.LockFailed;\n   275→    };\n   276→}\n   277→\n   278→fn tryLockExclusivePosix(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n   279→    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.EX | std.posix.LOCK.NB) catch |err| {\n   280→        // EWOULDBLOCK means lock is held by another process\n   281→        if (err == error.WouldBlock) {\n   282→            return false;\n   283→        }\n   284→        return error.LockFailed;\n   285→    };\n   286→    return true;\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→fn unlockPosix(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n   290→    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.UN) catch {\n   291→        return error.UnlockFailed;\n   292→    };\n   293→}\n   294→\n   295→// Windows implementation using LockFileEx\n   296→fn lockExclusiveWindows(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n   297→    const windows = std.os.windows;\n   298→    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n   299→\n   300→    // LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002\n   301→    const LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002;\n   302→    const result = windows.kernel32.LockFileEx(\n   303→        file.handle,\n   304→        LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK,\n   305→        0, // reserved\n   306→        1, // bytes to lock low\n   307→        0, // bytes to lock high\n   308→        &overlapped,\n   309→    );\n   310→\n   311→    if (result == 0) {\n   312→        return error.LockFailed;\n   313→    }\n   314→}\n   315→\n   316→fn tryLockExclusiveWindows(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n   317→    const windows = std.os.windows;\n   318→    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n   319→\n   320→    // LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002\n   321→    // LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY = 0x00000001\n   322→    const LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002;\n   323→    const LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY = 0x00000001;\n   324→    const result = windows.kernel32.LockFileEx(\n   325→        file.handle,\n   326→        LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK | LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY,\n   327→        0, // reserved\n   328→        1, // bytes to lock low\n   329→        0, // bytes to lock high\n   330→        &overlapped,\n   331→    );\n   332→\n   333→    if (result == 0) {\n   334→        const err = windows.kernel32.GetLastError();\n   335→        if (err == windows.Win32Error.ERROR_LOCK_VIOLATION) {\n   336→            return false;\n   337→        }\n   338→        return error.LockFailed;\n   339→    }\n   340→    return true;\n   341→}\n   342→\n   343→fn unlockWindows(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n   344→    const windows = std.os.windows;\n   345→    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n   346→\n   347→    const result = windows.kernel32.UnlockFileEx(\n   348→        file.handle,\n   349→        0, // reserved\n   350→        1, // bytes to unlock low\n   351→        0, // bytes to unlock high\n   352→        &overlapped,\n   353→    );\n   354→\n   355→    if (result == 0) {\n   356→        return error.UnlockFailed;\n   357→    }\n   358→}\n   359→\n   360→// PID management for stale lock detection\n   361→\n   362→/// Write the current process PID to the lock file.\n   363→fn writePidToLockFile(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n   364→    const pid = getCurrentPid();\n   365→    var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n   366→    const pid_str = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"{d}\\n\", .{pid}) catch return;\n   367→\n   368→    file.seekTo(0) catch return;\n   369→    file.writeAll(pid_str) catch return;\n   370→    file.sync() catch {};\n   371→}\n   372→\n   373→/// Read the holder PID from the lock file.\n   374→/// Returns null if the file is empty or contains invalid data.\n   375→fn readPidFromLockFile(file: std.fs.File) ?i32 {\n   376→    file.seekTo(0) catch return null;\n   377→\n   378→    var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n   379→    const bytes_read = file.read(&buf) catch return null;\n   380→\n   381→    if (bytes_read == 0) return null;\n   382→\n   383→    const content = buf[0..bytes_read];\n   384→    const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, content, \" \\t\\n\\r\");\n   385→    if (trimmed.len == 0) return null;\n   386→\n   387→    return std.fmt.parseInt(i32, trimmed, 10) catch null;\n   388→}\n   389→\n   390→/// Get the current process ID.\n   391→fn getCurrentPid() i32 {\n   392→    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n   393→        return @intCast(std.os.windows.kernel32.GetCurrentProcessId());\n   394→    } else if (builtin.os.tag == .linux) {\n   395→        return @bitCast(std.os.linux.getpid());\n   396→    } else {\n   397→        // macOS, FreeBSD, and other POSIX systems with libc\n   398→        return std.c.getpid();\n   399→    }\n   400→}\n   401→\n   402→/// Check if a process with the given PID is still alive.\n   403→fn isProcessAlive(pid: i32) bool {\n   404→    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n   405→        return isProcessAliveWindows(pid);\n   406→    } else {\n   407→        return isProcessAlivePosix(pid);\n   408→    }\n   409→}\n   410→\n   411→/// POSIX: Check if process is alive using kill(pid, 0).\n   412→fn isProcessAlivePosix(pid: i32) bool {\n   413→    // kill(pid, 0) checks if process exists without sending a signal\n   414→    // Returns 0 if process exists and we can send signals to it\n   415→    // Returns ESRCH if process doesn't exist\n   416→    // Returns EPERM if process exists but we can't signal it (still alive)\n   417→    const result = std.posix.kill(@intCast(pid), 0);\n   418→    return result != error.NoSuchProcess;\n   419→}\n   420→\n   421→/// Windows: Check if process is alive using OpenProcess.\n   422→fn isProcessAliveWindows(pid: i32) bool {\n   423→    const windows = std.os.windows;\n   424→\n   425→    // PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION = 0x1000\n   426→    const PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION = 0x1000;\n   427→\n   428→    const handle = windows.kernel32.OpenProcess(\n   429→        PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION,\n   430→        0, // bInheritHandle\n   431→        @intCast(pid),\n   432→    );\n   433→\n   434→    if (handle == null) {\n   435→        // Can't open process - true;\n   442→}\n   443→\n   444→// --- Tests ---\n   445→\n   446→test \"BeadsLock acquire and release\" {\n   447→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   448→    const test_dir = try File-based locking for concurrent write safety in beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Uses POSIX flock (or LockFileEx on Windows) for process-level locking.\n//! The lock is automatically released when the process terminates (kernel-managed).\n//!\n//! Stale lock detection:\n//! - PID is written to lock file after acquisition\n//! - Before blocking on a held lock, we check if the holder PID is still alive\n//! - If the holder process is dead, we break the stale lock safely\n//!\n//! Write path: flock(LOCK_EX) -> write PID -> operation -> flock(LOCK_UN) (~1ms)\n//! Lock is blocking by default, with optional timeout.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\npub const LockError = error{\n    LockFailed,\n    LockTimeout,\n    FileNotFound,\n    AccessDenied,\n    Unexpected,\n    StaleLockBroken,\n};\n\npub const BeadsLock = struct {\n    file: std.fs.File,\n    path: []const u8,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Default timeout for stale lock detection (30 seconds).\n    pub const DEFAULT_STALE_TIMEOUT_MS: u64 = 30_000;\n\n    /// Acquire exclusive lock. Blocks until available.\n    /// If the lock is held by a dead process, breaks the stale lock.\n    /// The lock is automatically released when the BeadsLock is deinitialized\n    /// or when release() is called.\n    pub fn acquire(path: []const u8) LockError!Self {\n        return acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path, DEFAULT_STALE_TIMEOUT_MS);\n    }\n\n    /// Acquire exclusive lock with stale lock detection and timeout.\n    /// If the lock holder process is dead, the lock is broken and acquired.\n    /// Returns error.LockTimeout if timeout_ms elapses without acquiring.\n    pub fn acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path: []const u8, timeout_ms: u64) LockError!Self {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        errdefer file.close();\n\n        // Try non-blocking lock first\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        if (locked) {\n            // Got the lock immediately - write our PID\n            writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n            return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n        }\n\n        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n            if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n                // Holder is dead - force acquire by blocking\n                // The kernel will grant us the lock since the holder is gone\n                lockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Holder is alive or PID unknown - wait with timeout\n        const start = std.time.milliTimestamp();\n        const deadline = start + @as(i64, @intCast(timeout_ms));\n\n        while (std.time.milliTimestamp() < deadline) {\n            const try_locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n            if (try_locked) {\n                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n            }\n\n            // Check if holder died while we were waiting\n            if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n                if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n                    // Holder died - try to acquire\n                    const dead_locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n                    if (dead_locked) {\n                        writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                        return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Sleep briefly before retrying\n            std.Thread.sleep(10 * std.time.ns_per_ms);\n        }\n\n        file.close();\n        return LockError.LockTimeout;\n    }\n\n    /// Try to acquire lock without blocking.\n    /// Returns null if lock is held by another process.\n    pub fn tryAcquire(path: []const u8) LockError!?Self {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        errdefer file.close();\n\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        if (!locked) {\n            file.close();\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Got the lock - write our PID\n        writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n\n        return .{\n            .file = file,\n            .path = path,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Try to acquire lock, breaking stale locks from dead processes.\n    /// Returns null if lock is held by a live process.\n    pub fn tryAcquireBreakingStale(path: []const u8) LockError!?Self {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        errdefer file.close();\n\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        if (locked) {\n            writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n            return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n        }\n\n        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n            if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n                // Holder is dead - force acquire\n                lockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Holder is alive\n        file.close();\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Acquire with timeout (in milliseconds).\n    /// Returns null if lock could not be acquired within timeout.\n    /// DEPRECATED: Use acquireWithStaleLockDetection instead for better stale lock handling.\n    pub fn acquireTimeout(path: []const u8, timeout_ms: u64) LockError!?Self {\n        const result = acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path, timeout_ms) catch |err| {\n            if (err == LockError.LockTimeout) {\n                return null;\n            }\n            return err;\n        };\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if this lock file appears to be held by a dead process.\n    /// This is informational only - use tryAcquireBreakingStale to actually acquire.\n    pub fn isStale(path: []const u8) bool {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return false;\n        defer file.close();\n\n        // Try to get lock - if we can, it's not held at all\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return false;\n        if (locked) {\n            unlock(file) catch {};\n            return false; // Not held, so not stale\n        }\n\n        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n            return !isProcessAlive(holder_pid);\n        }\n\n        // Can't determine PID, assume not stale\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the PID of the current lock holder, if available.\n    pub fn getHolderPid(path: []const u8) ?i32 {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return null;\n        defer file.close();\n        return readPidFromLockFile(file);\n    }\n\n    /// Release the lock.\n    pub fn release(self: *Self) void {\n        // Clear PID before releasing (optional, but clean)\n        self.file.seekTo(0) catch {};\n        self.file.setEndPos(0) catch {};\n\n        unlock(self.file) catch {};\n        self.file.close();\n    }\n\n    /// Deinitialize and release lock.\n    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n        self.release();\n    }\n};\n\n/// Execute a function while holding the beads lock.\n/// Provides RAII-style lock management.\npub fn withLock(path: []const u8, comptime func: fn () anyerror!void) !void {\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(path);\n    defer lock.release();\n    return func();\n}\n\n/// Execute a function with context while holding the beads lock.\npub fn withLockContext(\n    path: []const u8,\n    context: anytype,\n    comptime func: fn (@TypeOf(context)) anyerror!void,\n) !void {\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(path);\n    defer lock.release();\n    return func(context);\n}\n\n// Platform-specific implementations\n\nfn openOrCreateLockFile(path: []const u8) !std.fs.File {\n    const dir = std.fs.cwd();\n\n    // Ensure parent directory exists\n    if (std.fs.path.dirname(path)) |parent| {\n        dir.makePath(parent) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n            else => return err,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Open or create the lock file\n    return dir.createFile(path, .{\n        .read = true,\n        .truncate = false,\n        .lock = .none, // We handle locking separately\n    });\n}\n\nfn lockExclusive(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        try lockExclusiveWindows(file);\n    } else {\n        try lockExclusivePosix(file);\n    }\n}\n\nfn tryLockExclusive(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        return tryLockExclusiveWindows(file);\n    } else {\n        return tryLockExclusivePosix(file);\n    }\n}\n\nfn unlock(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        try unlockWindows(file);\n    } else {\n        try unlockPosix(file);\n    }\n}\n\n// POSIX implementation using flock\nfn lockExclusivePosix(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.EX) catch {\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    };\n}\n\nfn tryLockExclusivePosix(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.EX | std.posix.LOCK.NB) catch |err| {\n        // EWOULDBLOCK means lock is held by another process\n        if (err == error.WouldBlock) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    };\n    return true;\n}\n\nfn unlockPosix(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.UN) catch {\n        return error.UnlockFailed;\n    };\n}\n\n// Windows implementation using LockFileEx\nfn lockExclusiveWindows(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n\n    // LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002\n    const LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002;\n    const result = windows.kernel32.LockFileEx(\n        file.handle,\n        LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK,\n        0, // reserved\n        1, // bytes to lock low\n        0, // bytes to lock high\n        &overlapped,\n    );\n\n    if (result == 0) {\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    }\n}\n\nfn tryLockExclusiveWindows(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n\n    // LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002\n    // LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY = 0x00000001\n    const LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002;\n    const LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY = 0x00000001;\n    const result = windows.kernel32.LockFileEx(\n        file.handle,\n        LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK | LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY,\n        0, // reserved\n        1, // bytes to lock low\n        0, // bytes to lock high\n        &overlapped,\n    );\n\n    if (result == 0) {\n        const err = windows.kernel32.GetLastError();\n        if (err == windows.Win32Error.ERROR_LOCK_VIOLATION) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\nfn unlockWindows(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n\n    const result = windows.kernel32.UnlockFileEx(\n        file.handle,\n        0, // reserved\n        1, // bytes to unlock low\n        0, // bytes to unlock high\n        &overlapped,\n    );\n\n    if (result == 0) {\n        return error.UnlockFailed;\n    }\n}\n\n// PID management for stale lock detection\n\n/// Write the current process PID to the lock file.\nfn writePidToLockFile(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    const pid = getCurrentPid();\n    var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n    const pid_str = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"{d}\\n\", .{pid}) catch return;\n\n    file.seekTo(0) catch return;\n    file.writeAll(pid_str) catch return;\n    file.sync() catch {};\n}\n\n/// Read the holder PID from the lock file.\n/// Returns null if the file is empty or contains invalid data.\nfn readPidFromLockFile(file: std.fs.File) ?i32 {\n    file.seekTo(0) catch return null;\n\n    var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n    const bytes_read = file.read(&buf) catch return null;\n\n    if (bytes_read == 0) return null;\n\n    const content = buf[0..bytes_read];\n    const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, content, \" \\t\\n\\r\");\n    if (trimmed.len == 0) return null;\n\n    return std.fmt.parseInt(i32, trimmed, 10) catch null;\n}\n\n/// Get the current process ID.\nfn getCurrentPid() i32 {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        return @intCast(std.os.windows.kernel32.GetCurrentProcessId());\n    } else if (builtin.os.tag == .linux) {\n        return @bitCast(std.os.linux.getpid());\n    } else {\n        // macOS, FreeBSD, and other POSIX systems with libc\n        return std.c.getpid();\n    }\n}\n\n/// Check if a process with the given PID is still alive.\nfn isProcessAlive(pid: i32) bool {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        return isProcessAliveWindows(pid);\n    } else {\n        return isProcessAlivePosix(pid);\n    }\n}\n\n/// POSIX: Check if process is alive using kill(pid, 0).\nfn isProcessAlivePosix(pid: i32) bool {\n    // kill(pid, 0) checks if process exists without sending a signal\n    // Returns 0 if process exists and we can send signals to it\n    // Returns ESRCH if process doesn't exist\n    // Returns EPERM if process exists but we can't signal it (still alive)\n    const result = std.posix.kill(@intCast(pid), 0);\n    return result != error.NoSuchProcess;\n}\n\n/// Windows: Check if process is alive using OpenProcess.\nfn isProcessAliveWindows(pid: i32) bool {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n\n    // PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION = 0x1000\n    const PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION = 0x1000;\n\n    const handle = windows.kernel32.OpenProcess(\n        PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION,\n        0, // bInheritHandle\n        @intCast(pid),\n    );\n\n    if (handle == null) {\n        // Can't open process - assume it doesn't exist\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    // Process exists - close handle and return true\n    windows.CloseHandle(handle.?);\n    return true;\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"BeadsLock acquire and release\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_basic\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n    lock.release();\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock tryAcquire returns lock when available\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_try\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    var maybe_lock = try BeadsLock.tryAcquire(lock_path);\n    try std.testing.expect(maybe_lock != null);\n\n    if (maybe_lock) |*lock| {\n        lock.release();\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock deinit releases lock\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_deinit\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    {\n        var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n        defer lock.deinit();\n        // Lock is held here\n    }\n\n    // Lock should be released, can acquire again\n    var lock2 = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n    lock2.release();\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock acquireTimeout returns null on timeout\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_timeout\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    // Acquire first lock\n    var lock1 = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n    defer lock1.release();\n\n    // Try to acquire with short timeout - should fail\n    // Note: This test may be flaky in single-threaded test environment\n    // since we hold the lock in the same thread\n    // Skipping actual timeout test as it would hang\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock writes PID to lock file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_pid\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    // Acquire lock\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n\n    // Read the lock file to verify PID was written\n    const holder_pid = BeadsLock.getHolderPid(lock_path);\n    try std.testing.expect(holder_pid != null);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(getCurrentPid(), holder_pid.?);\n\n    lock.release();\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock.isStale returns false for live process\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_stale_live\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    // Acquire lock (held by current process, which is obviously alive)\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n    defer lock.release();\n\n    // isStale should return false since we're alive\n    // Note: We can't call isStale while holding the lock in same thread\n    // because the lock is held. This test verifies the API exists.\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock.getHolderPid returns null for empty lock file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_pid_empty\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    // Create empty lock file\n    const file = try std.fs.cwd().createFile(lock_path, .{});\n    file.close();\n\n    // getHolderPid should return null\n    const holder_pid = BeadsLock.getHolderPid(lock_path);\n    try std.testing.expect(holder_pid == null);\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock.tryAcquireBreakingStale works\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_break_stale\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    // Should acquire successfully when lock is not held\n    var maybe_lock = try BeadsLock.tryAcquireBreakingStale(lock_path);\n    try std.testing.expect(maybe_lock != null);\n\n    if (maybe_lock) |*lock| {\n        lock.release();\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"isProcessAlive returns true for current process\" {\n    const current_pid = getCurrentPid();\n    try std.testing.expect(isProcessAlive(current_pid));\n}\n\ntest \"isProcessAlive returns false for non-existent PID\" {\n    // Test with a PID that's very unlikely to exist.\n    // We try a range of high PIDs to find one that doesn't exist.\n    // This test is platform-dependent but should work on most systems.\n    var found_dead_pid = false;\n    var test_pid: i32 = 2147483600; // Start near max i32\n\n    // Try a few PIDs to find one that doesn't exist\n    while (test_pid < 2147483647 and !found_dead_pid) : (test_pid += 1) {\n        if (!isProcessAlive(test_pid)) {\n            found_dead_pid = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // We should be able to find at least one non-existent PID in this range\n    // If not, skip the test rather than fail (platform-specific behavior)\n    if (!found_dead_pid) {\n        // On some platforms, all PIDs in range might be considered \"alive\"\n        // due to kernel behavior. This is acceptable.\n        return;\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"readPidFromLockFile handles various formats\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_pid_formats\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    // Test with PID and newline\n    {\n        const file = try std.fs.cwd().createFile(lock_path, .{});\n        try file.writeAll(\"12345\\n\");\n        file.close();\n\n        const opened = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(lock_path, .{ .mode = .read_only });\n        defer opened.close();\n\n        const pid = readPidFromLockFile(opened);\n        try std.testing.expect(pid != null);\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 12345), pid.?);\n    }\n\n    // Test with PID only (no newline)\n    {\n        const file = try std.fs.cwd().createFile(lock_path, .{ .truncate = true });\n        try file.writeAll(\"67890\");\n        file.close();\n\n        const opened = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(lock_path, .{ .mode = .read_only });\n        defer opened.close();\n\n        const pid = readPidFromLockFile(opened);\n        try std.testing.expect(pid != null);\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 67890), pid.?);\n    }\n\n    // Test with whitespace\n    {\n        const file = try std.fs.cwd().createFile(lock_path, .{ .truncate = true });\n        try file.writeAll(\"  54321  \\n\");\n        file.close();\n\n        const opened = try std.fs.cwd().openFile(lock_path, .{ .mode = .read_only });\n        defer opened.close();\n\n        const pid = readPidFromLockFile(opened);\n        try std.testing.expect(pid != null);\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 54321), pid.?);\n    }\n\n    // Test with invalid content\n    {\n std.fs.cwd().openFile(lock_path, .{ .mode = .read_only });\n        defer opened.close();\n\n        const pid = readPidFromLockFile(opened);\n        try std.testing.expect(pid == null);\n    }\n}\n","numLines":681,"startLine":1,"totalLines":681}}}

std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n\n    const result = windows.kernel32.LockFileEx(\n        file.handle,\n        LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK | LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY,\n        0, // reserved\n        1, // bytes to lock low\n        0, // bytes to lock high\n        &overlapped,\n    );\n\n    if (result == 0) {\n        const err = windows.kernel32.GetLastError();\n        if (err == windows.Win32Error.ERROR_LOCK_VIOLATION) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    }\n    return true;\n}","originalFile":"//! File-based locking for concurrent write safety in beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Uses POSIX flock (or LockFileEx on Windows) for process-level locking.\n//! The lock is automatically released when the process terminates (kernel-managed).\n//!\n//! Stale lock detection:\n//! - PID is written to lock file after acquisition\n//! - Before blocking on a held lock, we check if the holder PID is still alive\n//! - If the holder process is dead, we break the stale lock safely\n//!\n//! Write path: flock(LOCK_EX) -> write PID -> operation -> flock(LOCK_UN) (~1ms)\n//! Lock is blocking by default, with optional timeout.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\npub const LockError = error{\n    LockFailed,\n    LockTimeout,\n    FileNotFound,\n    AccessDenied,\n    Unexpected,\n    StaleLockBroken,\n};\n\npub const BeadsLock = struct {\n    file: std.fs.File,\n    path: []const u8,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Default timeout for stale lock detection (30 seconds).\n    pub const DEFAULT_STALE_TIMEOUT_MS: u64 = 30_000;\n\n    /// Acquire exclusive lock. Blocks until available.\n    /// If the lock is held by a dead process, breaks the stale lock.\n    /// The lock is automatically released when the BeadsLock is deinitialized\n    /// or when release() is called.\n    pub fn acquire(path: []const u8) LockError!Self {\n        return acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path, DEFAULT_STALE_TIMEOUT_MS);\n    }\n\n    /// Acquire exclusive lock with stale lock detection and timeout.\n    /// If the lock holder process is dead, the lock is broken and acquired.\n    /// Returns error.LockTimeout if timeout_ms elapses without acquiring.\n    pub fn acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path: []const u8, timeout_ms: u64) LockError!Self {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        errdefer file.close();\n\n        // Try non-blocking lock first\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        if (locked) {\n            // Got the lock immediately - write our PID\n            writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n            return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n        }\n\n        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n            if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n                // Holder is dead - force acquire by blocking\n                // The kernel will grant us the lock since the holder is gone\n                lockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Holder is alive or PID unknown - wait with timeout\n        const start = std.time.milliTimestamp();\n        const deadline = start + @as(i64, @intCast(timeout_ms));\n\n        while (std.time.milliTimestamp() < deadline) {\n            const try_locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n            if (try_locked) {\n                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n            }\n\n            // Check if holder died while we were waiting\n            if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n                if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n                    // Holder died - try to acquire\n                    const dead_locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n                    if (dead_locked) {\n                        writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                        return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Sleep briefly before retrying\n            std.Thread.sleep(10 * std.time.ns_per_ms);\n        }\n\n        file.close();\n        return LockError.LockTimeout;\n    }\n\n    /// Try to acquire lock without blocking.\n    /// Returns null if lock is held by another process.\n    pub fn tryAcquire(path: []const u8) LockError!?Self {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        errdefer file.close();\n\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        if (!locked) {\n            file.close();\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Got the lock - write our PID\n        writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n\n        return .{\n            .file = file,\n            .path = path,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Try to acquire lock, breaking stale locks from dead processes.\n    /// Returns null if lock is held by a live process.\n    pub fn tryAcquireBreakingStale(path: []const u8) LockError!?Self {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        errdefer file.close();\n\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n        if (locked) {\n            writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n            return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n        }\n\n        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n            if (!isProcessAlive(holder_pid)) {\n                // Holder is dead - force acquire\n                lockExclusive(file) catch return LockError.LockFailed;\n                writePidToLockFile(file) catch {};\n                return .{ .file = file, .path = path };\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Holder is alive\n        file.close();\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Acquire with timeout (in milliseconds).\n    /// Returns null if lock could not be acquired within timeout.\n    /// DEPRECATED: Use acquireWithStaleLockDetection instead for better stale lock handling.\n    pub fn acquireTimeout(path: []const u8, timeout_ms: u64) LockError!?Self {\n        const result = acquireWithStaleLockDetection(path, timeout_ms) catch |err| {\n            if (err == LockError.LockTimeout) {\n                return null;\n            }\n            return err;\n        };\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if this lock file appears to be held by a dead process.\n    /// This is informational only - use tryAcquireBreakingStale to actually acquire.\n    pub fn isStale(path: []const u8) bool {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return false;\n        defer file.close();\n\n        // Try to get lock - if we can, it's not held at all\n        const locked = tryLockExclusive(file) catch return false;\n        if (locked) {\n            unlock(file) catch {};\n            return false; // Not held, so not stale\n        }\n\n        // Lock is held - check if holder is alive\n        if (readPidFromLockFile(file)) |holder_pid| {\n            return !isProcessAlive(holder_pid);\n        }\n\n        // Can't determine PID, assume not stale\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the PID of the current lock holder, if available.\n    pub fn getHolderPid(path: []const u8) ?i32 {\n        const file = openOrCreateLockFile(path) catch return null;\n        defer file.close();\n        return readPidFromLockFile(file);\n    }\n\n    /// Release the lock.\n    pub fn release(self: *Self) void {\n        // Clear PID before releasing (optional, but clean)\n        self.file.seekTo(0) catch {};\n        self.file.setEndPos(0) catch {};\n\n        unlock(self.file) catch {};\n        self.file.close();\n    }\n\n    /// Deinitialize and release lock.\n    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n        self.release();\n    }\n};\n\n/// Execute a function while holding the beads lock.\n/// Provides RAII-style lock management.\npub fn withLock(path: []const u8, comptime func: fn () anyerror!void) !void {\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(path);\n    defer lock.release();\n    return func();\n}\n\n/// Execute a function with context while holding the beads lock.\npub fn withLockContext(\n    path: []const u8,\n    context: anytype,\n    comptime func: fn (@TypeOf(context)) anyerror!void,\n) !void {\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(path);\n    defer lock.release();\n    return func(context);\n}\n\n// Platform-specific implementations\n\nfn openOrCreateLockFile(path: []const u8) !std.fs.File {\n    const dir = std.fs.cwd();\n\n    // Ensure parent directory exists\n    if (std.fs.path.dirname(path)) |parent| {\n        dir.makePath(parent) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n            else => return err,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Open or create the lock file\n    return dir.createFile(path, .{\n        .read = true,\n        .truncate = false,\n        .lock = .none, // We handle locking separately\n    });\n}\n\nfn lockExclusive(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        try lockExclusiveWindows(file);\n    } else {\n        try lockExclusivePosix(file);\n    }\n}\n\nfn tryLockExclusive(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        return tryLockExclusiveWindows(file);\n    } else {\n        return tryLockExclusivePosix(file);\n    }\n}\n\nfn unlock(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        try unlockWindows(file);\n    } else {\n        try unlockPosix(file);\n    }\n}\n\n// POSIX implementation using flock\nfn lockExclusivePosix(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.EX) catch {\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    };\n}\n\nfn tryLockExclusivePosix(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.EX | std.posix.LOCK.NB) catch |err| {\n        // EWOULDBLOCK means lock is held by another process\n        if (err == error.WouldBlock) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    };\n    return true;\n}\n\nfn unlockPosix(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    std.posix.flock(file.handle, std.posix.LOCK.UN) catch {\n        return error.UnlockFailed;\n    };\n}\n\n// Windows implementation using LockFileEx\nfn lockExclusiveWindows(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n\n    // LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002\n    const LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002;\n    const result = windows.kernel32.LockFileEx(\n        file.handle,\n        LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK,\n        0, // reserved\n        1, // bytes to lock low\n        0, // bytes to lock high\n        &overlapped,\n    );\n\n    if (result == 0) {\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    }\n}\n\nfn tryLockExclusiveWindows(file: std.fs.File) !bool {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n\n    // LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002\n    // LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY = 0x00000001\n    const LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK = 0x00000002;\n    const LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY = 0x00000001;\n    const result = windows.kernel32.LockFileEx(\n        file.handle,\n        LOCKFILE_EXCLUSIVE_LOCK | LOCKFILE_FAIL_IMMEDIATELY,\n        0, // reserved\n        1, // bytes to lock low\n        0, // bytes to lock high\n        &overlapped,\n    );\n\n    if (result == 0) {\n        const err = windows.kernel32.GetLastError();\n        if (err == windows.Win32Error.ERROR_LOCK_VIOLATION) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        return error.LockFailed;\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\nfn unlockWindows(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n    var overlapped: windows.OVERLAPPED = std.mem.zeroes(windows.OVERLAPPED);\n\n    const result = windows.kernel32.UnlockFileEx(\n        file.handle,\n        0, // reserved\n        1, // bytes to unlock low\n        0, // bytes to unlock high\n        &overlapped,\n    );\n\n    if (result == 0) {\n        return error.UnlockFailed;\n    }\n}\n\n// PID management for stale lock detection\n\n/// Write the current process PID to the lock file.\nfn writePidToLockFile(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    const pid = getCurrentPid();\n    var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n    const pid_str = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"{d}\\n\", .{pid}) catch return;\n\n    file.seekTo(0) catch return;\n    file.writeAll(pid_str) catch return;\n    file.sync() catch {};\n}\n\n/// Read the holder PID from the lock file.\n/// Returns null if the file is empty or contains invalid data.\nfn readPidFromLockFile(file: std.fs.File) ?i32 {\n    file.seekTo(0) catch return null;\n\n    var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n    const bytes_read = file.read(&buf) catch return null;\n\n    if (bytes_read == 0) return null;\n\n    const content = buf[0..bytes_read];\n    const trimmed = std.mem.trim(u8, content, \" \\t\\n\\r\");\n    if (trimmed.len == 0) return null;\n\n    return std.fmt.parseInt(i32, trimmed, 10) catch null;\n}\n\n/// Get the current process ID.\nfn getCurrentPid() i32 {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        return @intCast(std.os.windows.kernel32.GetCurrentProcessId());\n    } else if (builtin.os.tag == .linux) {\n        return @bitCast(std.os.linux.getpid());\n    } else {\n        // macOS, FreeBSD, and other POSIX systems with libc\n        return std.c.getpid();\n    }\n}\n\n/// Check if a process with the given PID is still alive.\nfn isProcessAlive(pid: i32) bool {\n    if (builtin.os.tag == .windows) {\n        return isProcessAliveWindows(pid);\n    } else {\n        return isProcessAlivePosix(pid);\n    }\n}\n\n/// POSIX: Check if process is alive using kill(pid, 0).\nfn isProcessAlivePosix(pid: i32) bool {\n    // kill(pid, 0) checks if process exists without sending a signal\n    // Returns 0 if process exists and we can send signals to it\n    // Returns ESRCH if process doesn't exist\n    // Returns EPERM if process exists but we can't signal it (still alive)\n    const result = std.posix.kill(@intCast(pid), 0);\n    return result != error.NoSuchProcess;\n}\n\n/// Windows: Check if process is alive using OpenProcess.\nfn isProcessAliveWindows(pid: i32) bool {\n    const windows = std.os.windows;\n\n    // PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION = 0x1000\n    const PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION = 0x1000;\n\n    const handle = windows.kernel32.OpenProcess(\n        PROCESS_QUERY_LIMITED_INFORMATION,\n        0, // bInheritHandle\n        @intCast(pid),\n    );\n\n    if (handle == null) {\n        // Can't open process - assume it doesn't exist\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    // Process exists - close handle and return true\n    windows.CloseHandle(handle.?);\n    return true;\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"BeadsLock acquire and release\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n    lock.release();\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    var maybe_lock = try BeadsLock.tryAcquire(lock_path);\n    try std.testing.expect(maybe_lock != null);\n\n    if (maybe_lock) |*lock| {\n        lock.release();\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock deinit releases lock\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"lock_deinit\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n    defer allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n    {\n        var lock = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n        defer lock.deinit();\n        // Lock is held here\n    }\n\n    // Lock should be released, can acquire again\n    var lock2 = try BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path);\n    lock2.release();\n}\n\ntest \"BeadsLock acquireTimeout returns null on timeout\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n // Start near max i32\n\n    // Try a few PIDs to find one that doesn't exist\n    while (test_pid < 2147483647 and !found_dead_pid) : (test_pid += 1) {\n        if (!isProcessAlive(test_pid)) {\n            found_dead_pid = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // We should be able to find at least one non-existent PID in this range\n    // If not, skip the test rather than fail (platform-specific behavior)\n    if (!found_dead_pid) {\n        // On some platforms, all PIDs in range might be considered \"alive\"\n        // due to kernel behavior. Add to ~/.bashrc: source <(bz completions bash)\n\n_bz_completions() {\n    local cur prev words cword\n    _init_completion || return\n\n    local commands=\"init create q show update close reopen delete list ready blocked search stale count dep label comments history audit sync config info stats doctor version schema completions\"\n\n    if [[ $cword -eq 1 ]]; then\n        COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$commands\" -- \"$cur\"))\n        return\n    fi\n\n    case ${words[1]} in\n        show|update|close|reopen|delete|comments|history)\n            # Complete with issue IDs\n            local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        dep)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list tree cycles\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        label)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list list-all\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        comments)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add list\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        config)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"get set list\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            fi\n            ;;\n        sync)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--flush-only --import-only\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        completions)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"bash zsh fish powershell\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        create)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"--priority --type
